class="TypographyStyle-sc-11lquxl itzVHH">Privacy Policy</span></nav></div><main class="PageStyle-sc-13qqs4t bxFYvq"><div class="GridItemStyle-sc-1uambol gDESlB"><div class="Wrapper-sc-gehxp6 bPQbdx"><div class="sc-AxjAm cIWfZS"><div class="sc-AxjAm bZqxgW"><div class="sc-AxjAm glyMyi"><h3 class="TypographyStyle-sc-11lquxl bmpVjT">POLICIES</h3><p class="TypographyStyle-sc-11lquxl eAZhOD">Privacy Policy</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="GridWrapper-sc-z19qw0 erNiQh"><div class="GridOffset-sc-1mxgq9x kgxYjn"><div class="GridItemStyle-sc-1uambol bBAazv"><div class="Wrapper-sc-gehxp6 bPQbdx"><div class="GridWrapper-sc-z19qw0 ipDRTs privacyPolicyPageWrapper"><div class="GridOffset-sc-1mxgq9x kgxYjn"><div class="GridItemStyle-sc-1uambol gDESlB"><div class="Wrapper-sc-gehxp6 bPQbdx"><div class="ContentWrapper-sc-wfvc9v gkuWqg"><p class="TypographyStyle-sc-11lquxl gVBKsR privacyPolicyText">Effective Date: January 1, 2020</p>
<p class="TypographyStyle-sc-11lquxl gVBKsR privacyPolicyText">Intermatic, Inc. respects your privacy and is committed to protecting it through compliance with this Privacy Policy. We have created this Privacy Policy to inform you of how we collect, use and protect your personal information.</p>
<p class="TypographyStyle-sc-11lquxl gVBKsR privacyPolicyText">We collect information from you when you visit our website (Intermatic.com), register on our site/portal, fill out a form or download a mobile app. When ordering or registering on our site or on our app, as appropriate, you may be asked to enter your personal contact information.</p>
<p class="TypographyStyle-sc-11lquxl gVBKsR privacyPolicyPoints">Types of information that we may collect:</p>
<ul class="UnorderedList-sc-1gl7lfr iMchvn privacyPolicyPoints-ul">
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">Contact details, such as name, email address, postal address and telephone number.</li>
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">Professional information.</li>
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">Payment information, such as a credit or debit card number or bank account details.</li>
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">Comments, feedback, posts and other content submitted, including survey information.</li>
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">Interests and communication preferences including marketing permissions where appropriate.</li>
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">Location information such as provided through a mobile app.</li>
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">Voice recordings, and copies of your correspondence (including email addresses), if you contact us.</li>
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">Website and communication usage information, such as correspondence and details of your use of our website and services obtained through cookies or other tracking technologies.</li>
</ul>
<p class="TypographyStyle-sc-11lquxl gVBKsR privacyPolicyPoints-ways">Any of the information we collect from you may be used in one of the following ways:</p>
<ul class="UnorderedList-sc-1gl7lfr iMchvn privacyPolicyPoints-ul-info">
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">To personalize your experience. Your information helps us to better respond to your individual needs and requirements.</li>
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">To improve our web site. We continually strive to improve our web site offerings based on the information and feedback we receive from you.</li>
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">To improve customer service. Your information helps us to more effectively respond to your customer service requests and support needs.</li>
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">To process transactions. Your information, whether public or private, will not be sold, exchanged, transferred, or given to any other company for any reason whatsoever, without your consent, other than for the express purpose of delivering products or services requested by you.</li>
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">To send periodic e-mails. The e-mail address you provide for order processing or product notifications, may be used to send you information and updates pertaining to your requests, in addition to receiving occasional company news, updates, related product or service information, etc. Note: if at any time you would like to unsubscribe from receiving future e-mails, we include detailed unsubscribe instructions at the bottom of any e-mail we send.</li>
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">To administer an event, contest, promotion, survey, or other site feature.</li>
<li class="ListItem-sc-1ki5k3p gSKIUI privacyPolicyPoints-li">To determine location information such as provided through a mobile app.</li>
</ul>
<p class="TypographyStyle-sc-11lquxl gVBKsR privacyPolicy-personalInfo">How we secure personal information:</p>
<p class="TypographyStyle-sc-11lquxl gVBKsR privacyPolicyText-personalInfo">We have implemented generally accepted standards of technology and operational security to protect personal data from loss, misuse, alteration, or destruction. Only authorized persons are provided access to personally identifiable information collected.</p>
<p class="TypographyStyle-sc-11lquxl gVBKsR"></p>
<p class="TypographyStyle-sc-11lquxl gVBKsR privacyPolicyText-personalInfo2">Although we use appropriate security measures once we have received your personal data, the transmission of data over the internet (including by e-mail) is never completely secure. We endeavor to protect personal data, but we cannot guarantee the security of data transmitted to or by us.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div
